If sink or audit policy is nil, no decoration takes place.\n42: func WithAudit(handler http.Handler, sink audit.Sink, policy audit.PolicyRuleEvaluator, longRunningCheck request.LongRunningRequestCheck) http.Handler {\n43: \tif sink == nil || policy == nil {\n44: \t\treturn handler\n45: \t}\n46: \treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {\n47: \t\tac, err := evaluatePolicyAndCreateAuditEvent(req, policy, sink)\n48: \t\tif err != nil {\n49: \t\t\tutilruntime.HandleError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create audit event: %v\", err))\n50: \t\t\tresponsewriters.InternalError(w, req, errors.New(\"failed to create audit event\"))\n51: \t\t\treturn\n52: \t\t}\n53: \n54: \t\tif !ac.Enabled() {\n55: \t\t\thandler.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n56: \t\t\treturn\n57: \t\t}\n58: \n59: \t\tctx := req.Context()\n60: \n61: \t\tif processed := ac.ProcessEventStage(ctx, auditinternal.StageRequestReceived); !processed {\n62: \t\t\taudit.ApiserverAuditDroppedCounter.WithContext(ctx).Inc()\n63: \t\t\tresponsewriters.InternalError(w, req, errors.New(\"failed to store audit event\"))\n64: \t\t\treturn\n65: \t\t}\n66: \n67: \t\t// intercept the status code\n68: \t\tisLongRunning := false\n69: \t\tif longRunningCheck != nil {\n70: \t\t\tri, _ := request.RequestInfoFrom(ctx)\n71: \t\t\tif longRunningCheck(req, ri) {\n72: \t\t\t\tisLongRunning = true\n73: \t\t\t}\n74: \t\t}\n75: \t\trespWriter := decorateResponseWriter(ctx, w, isLongRunning)\n76: \n77: \t\t// send audit event when we leave this func, either via a panic or cleanly. Sets the Audit-ID response header.\\n\\n## Audit Event Creation and Request Logging\\n- **WithAudit** (audit.go): Main HTTP middleware that decorates the request/response lifecycle. Evaluates the audit policy, creates audit events, and sends them through stages (RequestReceived, ResponseStarted, ResponseComplete, Panic).\\n- **AuditContext** (context.go): Holds the audit event being constructed during the request. Manages the event state and processes different audit stages through the configured sink.\\n- **LogRequestMetadata** (request.go): Captures request metadata (URI, user, source IP, verb, object reference) into the audit event.\\n- **LogRequestObject** and **LogResponseObject** (request.go): Capture the actual request/response bodies when audit level is Metadata or higher.\\n\\n## Audit Policy Evaluation\\n- **PolicyRuleEvaluator** interface (evaluator.go): Defines methods for evaluating audit policy rules against request attributes.\\n- **NewPolicyRuleEvaluator** (policy/checker.go): Creates a policy evaluator that matches requests against policy rules and returns RequestAuditConfig (audit level, omit stages, omit managed fields).\\n- **LoadPolicyFromFile** and **LoadPolicyFromBytes** (policy/reader.go): Load and parse the audit policy YAML/JSON configuration file.\\n\\n## Authentication Failure Audit\\n- **WithFailedAuthenticationAudit** (authn_audit.go): Specialized middleware for logging failed authentication attempts.\\n\\n## Audit Backend Dispatch and Processing\\n- **Backend** and **Sink** interfaces (types.go): Define the contract for audit event processors.\\n- **Union** (union.go): Dispatcher that sends audit events to multiple backends (e.g., both file and webhook).\\n\\n## Backend Implementations\\n- **Log Backend** (log/backend.go): Writes audit events to a file in JSON or legacy text format.\\n- **Webhook Backend** (webhook/webhook.go): Sends audit events to an external HTTP webhook endpoint with exponential backoff retry.\\n- **Buffered Backend** (buffered/buffered.go): Batches events before sending to a delegate backend, with rate limiting and async processing options.\\n- **Truncate Backend** (truncate/truncate.go): Wraps another backend and removes large request/response objects if events exceed size limits, keeping metadata intact.\\n\\n## Configuration and Integration\\n- **AuditOptions** (server/options/audit.go): Orchestrates the creation of all audit components, reads configuration flags, builds the policy evaluator, and chains backends together (truncate → log/webhook).\\n\\n## Admission and Response Handling\\n- **WithAudit** in admission (admission/audit.go): Captures audit annotations from admission controllers.\\n- **decorateResponseWriter** (audit.go): Intercepts response writes to capture status codes and response bodies for audit logging.\\n\\n## The Complete Request Flow\\n1. WithAuditInit initializes context with audit ID\\n2. WithAudit evaluates policy and starts RequestReceived stage\\n3. Request handlers are invoked, logging request metadata, objects, and annotations\\n4. Response is captured by decorated writer\\n5. ResponseStarted and ResponseComplete stages process events\\n6. Events flow through Union → [Truncate] → [Log/Webhook backends]\\n7. Truncate backend removes large bodies if needed\\n8. Log backend writes to files, Webhook backend sends to external endpoints\\n9. packages in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/. Here's the complete flow:\\n\\n## Audit Initialization\\n- **WithAuditInit** (audit_init.go): Creates the audit context and generates a unique audit ID for each request. Sets the Audit-ID response header.\\n\\n## Audit Event Creation and Request Logging\\n- **WithAudit** (audit.go): Main HTTP middleware that decorates the request/response lifecycle. Evaluates the audit policy, creates audit events, and sends them through stages (RequestReceived, ResponseStarted, ResponseComplete, Panic).\\n- **AuditContext** (context.go): Holds the audit event being constructed during the request. Manages the event state and processes different audit stages through the configured sink.\\n- **LogRequestMetadata** (request.go): Captures request metadata (URI, user, source IP, verb, object reference) into the audit event.\\n- **LogRequestObject** and **LogResponseObject** (request.go): Capture the actual request/response bodies when audit level is Metadata or higher.\\n\\n## Audit Policy Evaluation\\n- **PolicyRuleEvaluator** interface (evaluator.go): Defines methods for evaluating audit policy rules against request attributes.\\n- **NewPolicyRuleEvaluator** (policy/checker.go): Creates a policy evaluator that matches requests against policy rules and returns RequestAuditConfig (audit level, omit stages, omit managed fields).\\n- **LoadPolicyFromFile** and **LoadPolicyFromBytes** (policy/reader.go): Load and parse the audit policy YAML/JSON configuration file.\\n\\n## Authentication Failure Audit\\n- **WithFailedAuthenticationAudit** (authn_audit.go): Specialized middleware for logging failed authentication attempts.\\n\\n## Audit Backend Dispatch and Processing\\n- **Backend** and **Sink** interfaces (types.go): Define the contract for audit event processors.\\n- **Union** (union.go): Dispatcher that sends audit events to multiple backends (e.g., both file and webhook).\\n\\n## Backend Implementations\\n- **Log Backend** (log/backend.go): Writes audit events to a file in JSON or legacy text format.\\n- **Webhook Backend** (webhook/webhook.go): Sends audit events to an external HTTP webhook endpoint with exponential backoff retry.\\n- **Buffered Backend** (buffered/buffered.go): Batches events before sending to a delegate backend, with rate limiting and async processing options.\\n- **Truncate Backend** (truncate/truncate.go): Wraps another backend and removes large request/response objects if events exceed size limits, keeping metadata intact.\\n\\n## Configuration and Integration\\n- **AuditOptions** (server/options/audit.go): Orchestrates the creation of all audit components, reads configuration flags, builds the policy evaluator, and chains backends together (truncate → log/webhook).\\n\\n## Admission and Response Handling\\n- **WithAudit** in admission (admission/audit.go): Captures audit annotations from admission controllers.\\n- **decorateResponseWriter** (audit.go): Intercepts response writes to capture status codes and response bodies for audit logging.\\n\\n## The Complete Request Flow\\n1. WithAuditInit initializes context with audit ID\\n2. WithAudit evaluates policy and starts RequestReceived stage\\n3. Request handlers are invoked, logging request metadata, objects, and annotations\\n4. Response is captured by decorated writer\\n5. ResponseStarted and ResponseComplete stages process events\\n6. Events flow through Union → [Truncate] → [Log/Webhook backends]\\n7. Truncate backend removes large bodies if needed\\n8. Log backend writes to files, Webhook backend sends to external endpoints\\n9. Buffered wrapper adds batching, rate limiting, and async processing\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
